<h1 _ngcontent-gkh-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="TextReader（朗读控件）"> TextReader（朗读控件） </h1>

<div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>朗读控件使用AI能力将文本实时转化成语音并进行朗读，适用于一些新闻类文本内容浏览类APP，帮助用户在一些无法直接浏览文本内容的场景下，通过文本朗读来高效获取信息。</p>    <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="section10727191484112" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section10727191484112" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-gkh-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" class="hljs-string">'@kit.SpeechKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="section928783510820" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">注意事项<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section928783510820" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>调用朗读控件接口前，必须先调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-textreader-api#section173751154134515">init</a>初始化，否则会报错。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1190px;">     <h2 id="section173751154134515" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">init<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section173751154134515" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>init(context: common.BaseContext, readParams: ReaderParam): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>朗读控件初始化，用于初始化TTS引擎和底层播放器，初始化失败会返回对应错误码。</p>     <p>使用Promise异步回调。若要配置长时权限，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/speech-textreader-guide#li56192364816" target="_blank">开发指南步骤9</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.KEEP_BACKGROUND_RUNNING</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.10.1.5.1.1" width="30.826917308269174%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.10.1.5.1.2" width="30.826917308269174%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.10.1.5.1.3" width="9.199080091990801%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.10.1.5.1.4" width="29.14708529147085%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.826917308269174%">          <p>context</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.826917308269174%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-application-basecontext" target="_blank">common.BaseContext</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="9.199080091990801%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.14708529147085%">          <p>当前应用上下文</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.826917308269174%">          <p>readParams</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.826917308269174%">          <p><a      <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.14708529147085%">          <p>朗读参数</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>Promise&lt;void&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>Promise对象。无返回结果的Promise对象。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-errorcode">ArkTS API错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.15.1.3.1.1" class="cellrowborder" width="30.869999999999997%">          <p>201</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="69.13%">          <p>Permission denied. Interface caller does not have permission ohos.permission.KEEP_BACKGROUND_RUNNING.</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.869999999999997%"> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2403px;">     <h2 id="section143611912403" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">start<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section143611912403" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>start(readInfoList: ReadInfo[], articleId?: string): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>朗读控件起播。播放失败返回对应错误码。</p>     <p>使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.1" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.2" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>readInfoList</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-textreader-api#section129918404172">ReadInfo</a>[]</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>播放文章列表</p>          <ul>           <li>若列表的第一篇文章是有分类的（即带有category或categoryObject字段），后续文章不带分类，也会归为“其他”分类下</li>           <li>若列表的第一篇是没有分类的，后续文章即使带分类，也不会生效</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>articleId</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>文章id，articleId不传时，默认从文章列表中的第一篇开始播放；传参时，从传入articleId对应的文章开始依次往下播放。（文章id不能重复，否则从列表进入同id的文章，会自动选择同id的第一篇朗读）</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr width="50%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>Promise&lt;void&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2544px;">     <h2 id="section147237941810" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">start<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section147237941810" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>start(readInfoList: ReadInfo[], articleId: string | undefined, startParams: StartParams): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>朗读控件起播，可以通过设置startParams参数实现隐藏Minibar等效果。播放失败返回对应错误码。</p>     <p>使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.2(14)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.1" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.2" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>readInfoList</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p><a    <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>播放文章列表</p>          <ul>           <li>若列表的第一篇文章是有分类的（即带有category或categoryObject字段），后续文章不带分类，也会归为“其他”分类下</li>           <li>若列表的第一篇是没有分类的，后续文章即使带分类，也不会生效</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>articleId</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>string | undefined</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>文章id（文章id不能重复，否则从列表进入同id的文章，会自动选择同id的第一篇文章），articleId不传时，默认从文章列表中的第一篇开始播放；传参时，从传入articleId对应的文章开始依次往下播放</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>      <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>朗读控件起播参数</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">loadMore<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1736815283116" <p>加载更多文章到文章列表。需在项目init和start之后调用，建议在'requestMore'操作监听中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1262px;">     <h2 id="section19795822172419" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">on(type: 'setArticle')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section19795822172419" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span 'setArticle', callback: Callback&lt;string&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册设置文章回调函数，点击文章或者切换文章时，若目标文章内容为空（bodyInfo值为空）时，触发该回调执行。同一类型监听，注册多个回调函数，仅第一次注册有效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div id="mcps1.3.25.8.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.8.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%"> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1214px;">     <h2 id="section535020196399" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">off(type: 'setArticle')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" 'setArticle', callback?: Callback&lt;string&gt;): void</p>     <p>在on(type: 'setArticle')函数调用之后使用，用于注销设置文章回调函数。注销监听后，可以重新注册。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p>注册点击事件回调函数，点击标题、作者、通知栏时，触发该回调执行。同一类型监听，注册多个回调函数，仅第一次注册有效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1406px;">     <h2 id="section5929175119371" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">off(type: 'clickArticle' | 'clickAuthor' | 'clickNotification')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section5929175119371" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>off(type: 'clickArticle' | 'clickAuthor' | 'clickNotification', callback?: Callback&lt;string&gt;): void</p>     <p>在on(type: 'clickArticle' | 'clickAuthor' | 'clickNotification')函数调用之后使用，用于注销点击事件回调函数。注销监听后，可以重新注册。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.8.1.5.1.1" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.8.1.5.1.2" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.8.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.8.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>type</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>事件回调类型</p>          <ul>           <li>'clickArticle'：点击文章标题，取消回调</li>           <li>'clickAuthor'：点击作者事件，取消回调</li>           <li>'clickNotification'：点击通知栏事件，取消回调</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>callback</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>Callback&lt;string&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>需要取消监听的回调函数，需与订阅时传入的回调函数是同一个，若不填，则取消当前应用监听该事件的所有回调函数（当前仅有一个）。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-errorcode">ArkTS API错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1326px;">     <h2 id="section4889437173513" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">on(type: 'showPanel' | 'hidePanel')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section4889437173513" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span 'showPanel' | 'hidePanel', callback: Callback&lt;void&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册拉起/收回播放面板回调函数，拉起/收回播放面板时，触发该回调执行。同一类型监听，注册多个回调函数，仅第一次注册有效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div id="mcps1.3.29.8.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.8.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%"> active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1444125912412" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span 'stop' | 'release', callback: Callback&lt;void&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册停止/释放回调函数，调用stop/release时，触发该回调执行。同一类型监听，注册多个回调函数，仅第一次注册有效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.8.1.5.1.1" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.8.1.5.1.2" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.8.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.8.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>type</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>事件回调类型</p>          <ul>           <li>'stop'：调用stop接口</li>           <li>'release'：调用release释放资源</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>callback</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>Callback&lt;void&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>stop/release事件回调函数</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-errorcode">ArkTS API错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1278px;">     <h2 id="section951610492448" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">off(type: 'stop' | 'release')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section951610492448" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>off(type: 'stop' | 'release', callback?: Callback&lt;void&gt;): void</p>     <p>在on(type: 'stop' | 'release')函数调用之后使用，用于注销stop/release事件的回调函数。注销监听后，可以重新注册。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.8.1.5.1.1" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.8.1.5.1.2" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.8.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.8.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>type</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>事件回调类型</p>          <ul>           <li>'stop'：调用stop接口或用户主动滑动通知栏退出</li>           <li>'release'：调用release释放资源</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>callback</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>Callback&lt;void&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>需要取消监听的回调函数，需与订阅时传入的回调函数是同一个，若不填，则取消当前应用监听该事件的所有回调函数（当前仅有一个）。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a 'stateChange', callback: Callback&lt;ReadState&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册状态变化回调函数，当前正在播放的文章状态变更时，触发该回调执行。同一类型监听，注册多个回调函数，仅第一次注册有效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> 'requestMore', callback: Callback&lt;void&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册请求更多文章回调函数，拉到播放列表底端或播放到文章最后一篇，触发该回调执行。同一类型监听，注册多个回调函数，仅第一次注册有效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>需要取消监听的回调函数，需与订阅时传入的回调函数是同一个。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-errorcode">ArkTS API错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1398px;">     <h2 id="section2382121555318" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">on(type: 'eventNotification' | 'eventPanel')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section2382121555318" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>on(type: 'eventNotification' | 'eventPanel', callback: Callback&lt;NotificationEvent| PanelEvent&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册播控中心/播放面板状态回调函数，播控中心/播放面板状态发生变化时，触发该回调执行。同一类型监听，注册多个回调函数，仅第一次注册有效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>  <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>播控中心/播放面板状态发生变化时，触发该回调执行。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1302px;">     <h2 id="section11550141725715" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">off(type: 'eventNotification' | 'eventPanel')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section11550141725715" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>off(type: 'eventNotification' | 'eventPanel', callback?: Callback&lt;NotificationEvent | PanelEvent&gt;): void</p>     <p>在on(type: 'eventNotification' | 'eventPanel')函数调用之后使用，用于注销播控中心、播放面板状态发生变化的回调函数。注销监听后，可以重新注册。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.8.1.5.1.1" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.8.1.5.1.2" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.8.1.5.1.3" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.8.1.5.1.4" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>type</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>事件回调类型</p>          <ul>           <li>'eventNotification'：播控中心状态变化</li>           <li>'eventPanel'：播放面板状态变化</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>callback</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>Callback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-textreader-api#section1612119431629">NotificationEvent</a> | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-textreader-api#section13718113213211">PanelEvent</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.519248075192479%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.82691730826917%">          <p>需要取消监听的回调函数，需与订阅时传入的回调函数是同一个，若不填，则取消当前应用监听该事件的所有回调函数（当前仅有一个）。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/speech-errorcode">ArkTS style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1238px;">     <h2 id="section6867019205916" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">on(type: 'eventReadList')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" 'eventReadList', callback?: Callback&lt;Array&lt;ListEventState&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>在on(type: 'eventReadList')函数调用之后使用，用于注销播报列表相关事件的回调函数。注销监听后，可以重新注册。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>    <h2 id="section6549172112810" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">ReadProgressType<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section6549172112810" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>用于确定已播报时长上报类型的枚举类。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AI.Component.TextReader</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.2(14)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div
